I've uploaded a code repository in the directory /testbed. Consider the following PR description:

<pr_description>
bug: [GC] WasmEdge crash: `ref.test`/`ref.cast` on default-initialized local with concrete ref type
### Summary

# WasmEdge SIGSEGV: `ref.test`/`ref.cast` on default-initialized local with concrete ref type

## Version

- WasmEdge `77c5238980b3c9cd8fc7e7dc69b20127d9fd68ca` (includes fix from #4764)
- Linux 5.15.0-168-generic x86\_64

## Relation to #4757 / #4764

This is the **same crash site** as #4757 (`runRefTestOp` null-pointer dereference in `refInstr.cpp:339`), but a **different source** of the concrete-typed null. PR #4764 fixed the table-initialization path; this bug is in the **function-local initialization** path and remains unfixed on current `master`.

## Minimal Reproducer

```wat
(module
  (type $s (struct))
  (func (export "run")
    (local (ref null $s))
    local.get 0
    ref.test (ref null $s)
    drop
  )
)
```

```bash
wasm-tools parse crash.wat -o crash.wasm
wasm-tools validate crash.wasm   # OK
wasmedge crash.wasm run          # Segmentation fault
wasmtime run --wasm gc --invoke run crash.wasm  # OK
```

## (Potential) Root Cause

`ValueFromType` ([include/common/types.h:680](https://github.com/WasmEdge/WasmEdge/blob/77c5238980b3c9cd8fc7e7dc69b20127d9fd68ca/include/common/types.h#L680)) initializes reference-typed locals with `RefVariant(Type)`, passing the **raw concrete type** (e.g. `(ref null $s)`). This creates a null `RefVariant` whose `ValType` has `HTCode = TypeIndex`, violating the invariant that null references always carry abstract heap types.

When `ref.test` or `ref.cast` later calls `runRefTestOp` ([lib/executor/engine/refInstr.cpp:334-339](https://github.com/WasmEdge/WasmEdge/blob/77c5238980b3c9cd8fc7e7dc69b20127d9fd68ca/lib/executor/engine/refInstr.cpp#L334-L339)):

```cpp
if (!VT.isAbsHeapType()) {                       // true — TypeIndex is not abstract
    auto *Inst = Val.get<RefVariant>()
                    .getPtr<Runtime::Instance::CompositeBase>();
    // "Reference must not be nullptr here because the null references
    //  are typed with the least abstract heap type."
    if (Inst->getModule()) {                      // CRASH — Inst is nullptr
```

This is the same invariant violation fixed for tables in #4764, but through a different entry point.

Either normalize the type in `ValueFromType` (requires access to the module to call `toBottomType`), or normalize in `enterFunction` ([lib/executor/helper.cpp:212-216](https://github.com/WasmEdge/WasmEdge/blob/77c5238980b3c9cd8fc7e7dc69b20127d9fd68ca/lib/executor/helper.cpp#L212-L216)) where locals are pushed onto the stack — mirroring the approach used for tables in #4764.

## Acknowledgement

This bug was found during the development of GCsmith.

   307	    Runtime::StackManager &StackMgr, const uint32_t Cnt, const uint32_t TypeIdx,

   322	
   323	Expect<void>
   324	Executor::runRefTestOp(const Runtime::Instance::ModuleInstance *ModInst,
   325	                       ValVariant &Val, const AST::Instruction &Instr,
   326	                       const bool IsCast) const noexcept {
   327	  // Copy the value type here due to handling the externalized case.
   328	  auto VT = Val.get<RefVariant>().getType();
   329	  if (VT.isExternalized()) {
   330	    VT = ValType(VT.isNullableRefType() ? TypeCode::RefNull : TypeCode::Ref,
   331	                 TypeCode::ExternRef);
   332	  }
   333	  Span<const AST::SubType *const> GotTypeList = ModInst->getTypeList();
   334	  if (!VT.isAbsHeapType()) {
   335	    auto *Inst =
   336	        Val.get<RefVariant>().getPtr<Runtime::Instance::CompositeBase>();
   337	    // Reference must not be nullptr here because the null references are typed
   338	    // with the least abstract heap type.
   339	    if (Inst->getModule()) {
   340	      GotTypeList = Inst->getModule()->getTypeList();
   341	    }
   342	  }
   343	
   344	  if (AST::TypeMatcher::matchType(ModInst->getTypeList(), Instr.getValType(),
   345	                                  GotTypeList, VT)) {
   346	    if (!IsCast) {
   347	      Val.emplace<uint32_t>(1U);
   348	    }
   349	  } else {
   350	    if (IsCast) {
   351	      spdlog::error(ErrCode::Value::CastFailed);
   352	      spdlog::error(ErrInfo::InfoMismatch(Instr.getValType(), VT));
   353	      spdlog::error(
   354	          ErrInfo::InfoInstruction(Instr.getOpCode(), Instr.getOffset()));
   355	      return Unexpect(ErrCode::Value::CastFailed);
   356	    } else {
   357	      Val.emplace<uint32_t>(0U);
   358	    }
   359	  }
   360	  return {};
   361	}

   400	Runtime::Instance::ElementInstance *
   401	Executor::getElemInstByIdx(Runtime::StackManager &StackMgr,
   402	                           const uint32_t Idx) const {
   403	  const auto *ModInst = StackMgr.getModule();
   404	  // When top frame is dummy frame, cannot find instance.
   405	  if (unlikely(ModInst == nullptr)) {
   406	    return nullptr;
   407	  }
   408	  return ModInst->unsafeGetElem(Idx);
   409	}

   422	TypeCode Executor::toBottomType(Runtime::StackManager &StackMgr,
   423	                                const ValType &Type) const {
   424	  if (Type.isRefType()) {
   425	    if (Type.isAbsHeapType()) {
   426	      switch (Type.getHeapTypeCode()) {
   427	      case TypeCode::NullFuncRef:
   428	      case TypeCode::FuncRef:
   429	        return TypeCode::NullFuncRef;
   430	      case TypeCode::NullExternRef:
   431	      case TypeCode::ExternRef:
   432	        return TypeCode::NullExternRef;
   433	      case TypeCode::NullRef:
   434	      case TypeCode::AnyRef:
   435	      case TypeCode::EqRef:
   436	      case TypeCode::I31Ref:
   437	      case TypeCode::StructRef:
   438	      case TypeCode::ArrayRef:
   439	        return TypeCode::NullRef;
   440	      case TypeCode::NullExnRef:
   441	      case TypeCode::ExnRef:
   442	        return TypeCode::NullExnRef;
   443	      default:
   444	        assumingUnreachable();
   445	      }
   446	    } else {
   447	      const auto &CompType =
   448	          (*StackMgr.getModule()->getType(Type.getTypeIndex()))
   449	              ->getCompositeType();
   450	      if (CompType.isFunc()) {
   451	        return TypeCode::NullFuncRef;
   452	      } else {
   453	        return TypeCode::NullRef;
   454	      }
   455	    }

   460	
   461	void Executor::cleanNumericVal(ValVariant &Val,
   462	                               const ValType &Type) const noexcept {
   463	  if (Type.isNumType()) {
   464	    switch (Type.getCode()) {
   465	    case TypeCode::I32: {
   466	      uint32_t V = Val.get<uint32_t>();
   467	      Val.emplace<uint128_t>(static_cast<uint128_t>(0U));
   468	      Val.emplace<uint32_t>(V);
   469	      break;
   470	    }
   471	    case TypeCode::F32: {
   472	      float V = Val.get<float>();
   473	      Val.emplace<uint128_t>(static_cast<uint128_t>(0U));
   474	      Val.emplace<float>(V);
   475	      break;
   476	    }
   477	    case TypeCode::I64: {
   478	      uint64_t V = Val.get<uint64_t>();
   479	      Val.emplace<uint128_t>(static_cast<uint128_t>(0U));
   480	      Val.emplace<uint64_t>(V);

     1	// SPDX-License-Identifier: Apache-2.0
     2	// SPDX-FileCopyrightText: 2019-2024 Second State INC
     3	
     4	#include "executor/executor.h"
     5	
     6	#include <cstdint>
     7	
     8	namespace WasmEdge {
     9	namespace Executor {
    10	
    11	// Instantiate table instance. See "include/executor/executor.h".
    12	Expect<void> Executor::instantiate(Runtime::StackManager &StackMgr,
    13	                                   Runtime::Instance::ModuleInstance &ModInst,
    14	                                   const AST::TableSection &TabSec) {
    15	  // A frame with temp. module is pushed into the stack in caller.
    16	
    17	  // Iterate through the table segments to instantiate and initialize table
    18	  // instances.
    19	  for (const auto &TabSeg : TabSec.getContent()) {
    20	    if (TabSeg.getExpr().getInstrs().size() > 0) {
    21	      // Run initialize expression.
    22	      EXPECTED_TRY(runExpression(StackMgr, TabSeg.getExpr().getInstrs())
    23	                       .map_error([](auto E) {
    24	                         spdlog::error(
    25	                             ErrInfo::InfoAST(ASTNodeAttr::Expression));
    26	                         return E;
    27	                       }));
    28	      // Pop result from stack.
    29	      RefVariant InitTabValue = StackMgr.pop().get<RefVariant>();
    30	      // Create and add the table instance into the module instance.
    31	      ModInst.addTable(TabSeg.getTableType(), InitTabValue);
    32	    } else {
    33	      // No init expression case. Use the null reference to initialize.
    34	      // Normalize the type to the bottom abstract heap type so that null
    35	      // references always carry abstract types, as ref.cast/ref.test assume.
    36	      auto BotType = toBottomType(StackMgr, TabSeg.getTableType().getRefType());
    37	      RefVariant InitTabValue(ValType(TypeCode::RefNull, BotType));
    38	      ModInst.addTable(TabSeg.getTableType(), InitTabValue);
    39	    }
    40	  }
    41	  return {};
    42	}
    43	
    44	} // namespace Executor
    45	} // namespace WasmEdge
    46

USAGE
	./build/tools/wasmedge/wasmedge [SUBCOMMANDS] [OPTIONS] [--] WASM_OR_SO [ARG ...]

SUBCOMMANDS
	compile
		Wasmedge compiler subcommand
	run
		Wasmedge runtime tool subcommand

OPTIONS
	
-h|--help
		Show this help messages
	
-v|--version
		Show version information
	
--reactor
		Enable reactor mode. Reactor mode calls `_initialize` if exported.
	
--dir
		Binding directories into WASI virtual filesystem. Each directory can be
		specified as --dir `host_path`. You can also map a guest directory to a host
		directory by --dir `guest_path:host_path`, where `guest_path` specifies the
		path that will correspond to `host_path` for calls like `fopen` in the guest.
		The default permission is `readwrite`, however, you can use --dir
		`guest_path:host_path:readonly` to make the mapping directory become a read
		only mode.
	
--env
		Environ variables. Each variable can be specified as --env `NAME=VALUE`.
	
--enable-instruction-count
		Enable generating code for counting Wasm instructions executed.
	
--enable-gas-measuring
		Enable generating code for counting gas burned during execution.
	
--enable-time-measuring
		Enable generating code for counting time during execution.
	
--enable-all-statistics
		Enable generating code for all statistics options include instruction
		counting, gas measuring, and execution time
	
--enable-jit
		Enable Just-In-Time compiler for running WASM
	
--enable-coredump
		Enable coredump when WebAssembly enters a trap
	
--coredump-for-wasmgdb
		Enable coredump for wasm-gdb to debug
	
--force-interpreter
		Forcibly run WASM in interpreter mode.
	
--allow-af-unix
		Enable UNIX domain sockets
	
--wasm-1
		Set as WASM 1.0 standard.
	
--wasm-2
		Set as WASM 2.0 standard.
	
--wasm-3
		Set as WASM 3.0 standard (default).
	
--disable-import-export-mut-globals
		Disable Import/Export of mutable globals proposal
	
--disable-non-trap-float-to-int
		Disable Non-trapping float-to-int conversions proposal
	
--disable-sign-extension-operators
		Disable Sign-extension operators proposal
	
--disable-multi-value
		Disable Multi-value proposal

   305	Expect<void> Loader::loadType(AST::SubType &SType) {

   314	    SType.setFinal(true);
   315	    return loadCompositeType(SType.getCompositeType());

   331	    }));

   123	Expect<ValType> Loader::loadValType(ASTNodeAttr From, bool IsStorageType) {
   124	  // Peek the valtype code.
   125	  auto B = FMgr.peekByte();
   126	  if (unlikely(!B)) {
   127	    return logLoadError(B.error(), FMgr.getLastOffset(), From);
   128	  }
   129	
   130	  // Check the first byte for value type cases.
   131	  TypeCode Code = static_cast<TypeCode>(*B);
   132	  switch (Code) {
   133	  case TypeCode::V128:
   134	    if (!Conf.hasProposal(Proposal::SIMD)) {
   135	      return logNeedProposal(ErrCode::Value::MalformedValType, Proposal::SIMD,
   136	                             FMgr.getLastOffset(), From);
   137	    }
   138	    [[fallthrough]];
   139	  case TypeCode::I32:
   140	  case TypeCode::I64:
   141	  case TypeCode::F32:
   142	  case TypeCode::F64:
   143	    FMgr.readByte();
   144	    return ValType(Code);

   146	  case TypeCode::I16:

   148	    // in the parent scope.

   150	      return logLoadError(ErrCode::Value::MalformedValType, FMgr.getOffset(),

     9	// Load binary and decode HeapType. See "include/loader/loader.h".
    10	Expect<ValType> Loader::loadHeapType(TypeCode TC, ASTNodeAttr From) {
    11	  // Read the heap type code.
    12	  auto Val = FMgr.readS33();
    13	  if (unlikely(!Val)) {
    14	    return logLoadError(Val.error(), FMgr.getLastOffset(), From);
    15	  }
    16	
    17	  // The error code is different when the reference-types proposal turned off.
    18	  ErrCode::Value FailCode = Conf.hasProposal(Proposal::ReferenceTypes)
    19	                                ? ErrCode::Value::MalformedRefType
    20	                                : ErrCode::Value::MalformedElemType;
    21	
    22	  if (*Val < 0) {
    23	    if (*Val < -64) {
    24	      // For checking the invalid s33 value which is larger than 1 byte.
    25	      return logLoadError(FailCode, FMgr.getLastOffset(), From);
    26	    }
    27	    TypeCode HTCode =
    28	        static_cast<TypeCode>(static_cast<uint8_t>((*Val) & INT64_C(0x7F)));
    29	    switch (HTCode) {
    30	    case TypeCode::ExternRef:
    31	      // For the ref.func instruction, the immediate changed to store the heap
    32	      // type directly instead of the reference type after applying the
    33	      // typed function reference proposal. Therefore the reference-types
    34	      // proposal should be checked here.
    35	      if (!Conf.hasProposal(Proposal::ReferenceTypes)) {
    36	        return logNeedProposal(FailCode, Proposal::ReferenceTypes,
    37	                               FMgr.getLastOffset(), From);
    38	      }
    39	      [[fallthrough]];
    40	    case TypeCode::FuncRef:
    41	      if (!Conf.hasProposal(Proposal::ReferenceTypes) &&
    42	          !Conf.hasProposal(Proposal::BulkMemoryOperations)) {
    43	        return logNeedProposal(FailCode, Proposal::ReferenceTypes,
    44	                               FMgr.getLastOffset(), From);
    45	      }
    46	      return ValType(TC, HTCode);
    47	    case TypeCode::NullFuncRef:
    48	    case TypeCode::NullExternRef:
    49	    case TypeCode::NullRef:
    50	    case TypeCode::AnyRef:
    51	    case TypeCode::EqRef:
    52	    case TypeCode::I31Ref:
    53	    case TypeCode::StructRef:
    54	    case TypeCode::ArrayRef:
    55	      if (!Conf.hasProposal(Proposal::GC)) {
    56	        return logNeedProposal(FailCode, Proposal::GC, FMgr.getLastOffset(),
    57	                               From);
    58	      }
    59	      return ValType(TC, HTCode);
    60	    case TypeCode::NullExnRef:
    61	    case TypeCode::ExnRef:
    62	      if (!Conf.hasProposal(Proposal::ExceptionHandling)) {
    63	        return logNeedProposal(ErrCode::Value::MalformedValType,
    64	                               Proposal::ExceptionHandling,
    65	                               FMgr.getLastOffset(), From);
    66	      }
    67	      return ValType(TC, HTCode);
    68	    default:
    69	      return logLoadError(FailCode, FMgr.getLastOffset(), From);
    70	    }
    71	  } else {
    72	    // Type index case. Legal if the function reference proposal is enabled.
    73	    if (!Conf.hasProposal(Proposal::FunctionReferences)) {
    74	      return logNeedProposal(FailCode, Proposal::FunctionReferences,
    75	                             FMgr.getLastOffset(), From);
    76	    }
    77	    return ValType(TC, static_cast<uint32_t>(*Val));
    78	  }
    79	}
    80

    92	                                : ErrCode::Value::MalformedElemType;
    93	
    94	  // Check the first byte for reference type cases.
    95	  TypeCode Code = static_cast<TypeCode>(*B);
    96	  switch (Code) {
    97	  case TypeCode::ExternRef:
    98	    if (!Conf.hasProposal(Proposal::ReferenceTypes)) {
    99	      return logNeedProposal(FailCode, Proposal::ReferenceTypes,

    14	namespace WasmEdge {
    15	namespace Executor {
    16	
    17	Executor::SavedThreadLocal::SavedThreadLocal(
    18	    Executor &Ex, Runtime::StackManager &StackMgr,
    19	    const Runtime::Instance::FunctionInstance &Func) noexcept {
    20	  // Prepare the execution context.
    21	  auto *ModInst =
    22	      const_cast<Runtime::Instance::ModuleInstance *>(Func.getModule());
    23	  SavedThis = This;
    24	  This = &Ex;
    25	
    26	  SavedExecutionContext = ExecutionContext;
    27	  ExecutionContext.StopToken = &Ex.StopToken;
    28	  ExecutionContext.Memories = ModInst->MemoryPtrs.data();
    29	  ExecutionContext.Globals = ModInst->GlobalPtrs.data();
    30	  if (Ex.Stat) {
    31	    ExecutionContext.InstrCount = &Ex.Stat->getInstrCountRef();
    32	    ExecutionContext.CostTable = Ex.Stat->getCostTable().data();
    33	    ExecutionContext.Gas = &Ex.Stat->getTotalCostRef();
    34	    ExecutionContext.GasLimit = Ex.Stat->getCostLimit();
    35	  }
    36	
    37	  SavedCurrentStack = CurrentStack;
    38	  CurrentStack = &StackMgr;
    39	}
    40	
    41	Executor::SavedThreadLocal::~SavedThreadLocal() noexcept {
    42	  CurrentStack = SavedCurrentStack;
    43	  ExecutionContext = SavedExecutionContext;
    44	  This = SavedThis;
    45	}
    46	
    47	Expect<AST::InstrView::iterator>
    48	Executor::enterFunction(Runtime::StackManager &StackMgr,
    49	                        const Runtime::Instance::FunctionInstance &Func,
    50	                        const AST::InstrView::iterator RetIt, bool IsTailCall) {
    51	  // RetIt: the return position when the entered function returns.
    52	
    53	  // Check if the interruption occurs.
    54	  if (unlikely(StopToken.exchange(0, std::memory_order_relaxed))) {
    55	    spdlog::error(ErrCode::Value::Interrupted);
    56	    return Unexpect(ErrCode::Value::Interrupted);
    57	  }
    58	
    59	  // Get function type for the params and returns num.
    60	  const auto &FuncType = Func.getFuncType();
    61	  const uint32_t ArgsN = static_cast<uint32_t>(FuncType.getParamTypes().size());
    62	  const uint32_t RetsN =
    63	      static_cast<uint32_t>(FuncType.getReturnTypes().size());
    64	
    65	  // For the exception handler, remove the inactive handlers caused by the
    66	  // branches.
    67	  if (likely(RetIt)) {
    68	    StackMgr.removeInactiveHandler(RetIt - 1);
    69	  }
    70	
    71	  if (Func.isHostFunction()) {
    72	    // Host function case: Push args and call function.
    73	    auto &HostFunc = Func.getHostFunc();
    74	
    75	    // Generate CallingFrame from current frame.
    76	    // The module instance will be nullptr if current frame is a dummy frame.
    77	    // For this case, use the module instance of this host function.
    78	    const auto *ModInst = StackMgr.getModule();
    79	    if (ModInst == nullptr) {
    80	      ModInst = Func.getModule();
    81	    }
    82	    Runtime::CallingFrame CallFrame(this, ModInst);
    83	
    84	    // Push frame.
    85	    StackMgr.pushFrame(Func.getModule(), // Module instance
    86	                       RetIt,            // Return PC
    87	                       ArgsN,            // Only args, no locals in stack
    88	                       RetsN,            // Returns num
    89	                       IsTailCall        // For tail-call
    90	    );
    91	
    92	    // Do the statistics if the statistics turned on.
    93	    if (Stat) {
    94	      // Check host function cost.
    95	      if (unlikely(!Stat->addCost(HostFunc.getCost()))) {
    96	        spdlog::error(ErrCode::Value::CostLimitExceeded);
    97	        return Unexpect(ErrCode::Value::CostLimitExceeded);
    98	      }
    99	      // Start recording time of running host function.
   100	      Stat->stopRecordWasm();
   101	      Stat->startRecordHost();
   102	    }
   103	
   104	    // Call pre-host-function
   105	    HostFuncHelper.invokePreHostFunc();
   106	
   107	    // Run host function.
   108	    Span<ValVariant> Args = StackMgr.getTopSpan(ArgsN);
   109	    for (uint32_t I = 0; I < ArgsN; I++) {
   110	      // For the number type cases of the arguments, the unused bits should be
   111	      // erased due to the security issue.
   112	      cleanNumericVal(Args[I], FuncType.getParamTypes()[I]);
   113	    }
   114	    std::vector<ValVariant> Rets(RetsN);
   115	    auto Ret = HostFunc.run(CallFrame, std::move(Args), Rets);
   116	
   117	    // Call post-host-function
   118	    HostFuncHelper.invokePostHostFunc();
   119	
   120	    // Do the statistics if the statistics turned on.
   121	    if (Stat) {
   122	      // Stop recording time of running host function.
   123	      Stat->stopRecordHost();
   124	      Stat->startRecordWasm();
   125	    }
   126	
   127	    // Check the host function execution status.
   128	    if (!Ret) {
   129	      if (Ret.error() == ErrCode::Value::HostFuncError ||
   130	          Ret.error().getCategory() != ErrCategory::WASM) {
   131	        spdlog::error(Ret.error());
   132	      }
   133	      return Unexpect(Ret);
   134	    }
   135	
   136	    // Push returns back to stack.
   137	    for (auto &R : Rets) {
   138	      StackMgr.push(std::move(R));
   139	    }
   140	
   141	    // For host function case, the continuation will be the continuation from
   142	    // the popped frame.
   143	    return StackMgr.popFrame();
   144	  } else if (Func.isCompiledFunction()) {
   145	    // Compiled function case: Execute the function and jump to the
   146	    // continuation.
   147	
   148	    // Push frame.
   149	    StackMgr.pushFrame(Func.getModule(), // Module instance
   150	                       RetIt,            // Return PC
   151	                       ArgsN,            // Only args, no locals in stack
   152	                       RetsN,            // Returns num
   153	                       IsTailCall        // For tail-call
   154	    );
   155	
   156	    // Prepare arguments.
   157	    Span<ValVariant> Args = StackMgr.getTopSpan(ArgsN);
   158	    std::vector<ValVariant> Rets(RetsN);
   159	    SavedThreadLocal Saved(*this, StackMgr, Func);
   160	
   161	    ErrCode Err;
   162	    try {
   163	      // Get symbol and execute the function.
   164	      Fault FaultHandler;
   165	      uint32_t Code = PREPARE_FAULT(FaultHandler);
   166	      if (Code != 0) {
   167	        auto InnerStackTrace = FaultHandler.stacktrace();
   168	        {
   169	          std::array<void *, 256> Buffer;
   170	          auto OuterStackTrace = stackTrace(Buffer);
   171	          while (!OuterStackTrace.empty() && !InnerStackTrace.empty() &&
   172	                 InnerStackTrace[InnerStackTrace.size() - 1] ==
   173	                     OuterStackTrace[OuterStackTrace.size() - 1]) {
   174	            InnerStackTrace = InnerStackTrace.first(InnerStackTrace.size() - 1);
   175	            OuterStackTrace = OuterStackTrace.first(OuterStackTrace.size() - 1);
   176	          }
   177	        }
   178	        StackTraceSize =
   179	            compiledStackTrace(StackMgr, InnerStackTrace, StackTrace).size();
   180	        Err = ErrCode(static_cast<ErrCategory>(Code >> 24), Code);

    35	/// SIMD types definition.
    36	template <typename Ty, size_t TotalSize,
    37	          std::enable_if_t<(TotalSize % sizeof(Ty) == 0), int> = 0>
    38	#if defined(_MSC_VER) && !defined(__clang__)
    39	/// Because MSVC does not support [[gnu::vector_size(16)]] or
    40	/// __attribute__((vector_size(16)), we use this type to fill the gap.
    41	using SIMDArray = std::array<Ty, (TotalSize / sizeof(Ty))>;
    42	#else
    43	using SIMDArray [[gnu::vector_size(TotalSize)]] = Ty;
    44	#endif
    45	
    46	using int64x2_t = SIMDArray<int64_t, 16>;
    47	using uint64x2_t = SIMDArray<uint64_t, 16>;
    48	using int32x4_t = SIMDArray<int32_t, 16>;

    54	using doublex2_t = SIMDArray<double, 16>;
    55	using floatx4_t = SIMDArray<float, 16>;

    60	// The bit pattern of the value types:
    61	// -----------------------------------------------------------------------------
    62	//  byte | 0th  | 1st  |      2nd     |         3rd         |     4th ~ 7th
    63	// ------|-------------|--------------|---------------------|-------------------
    64	//       |             | ValTypeCode  |         For the HeapType use
    65	//       |   0th:      | 0x7F, 0x7E,  | (Function references and GC proposal)
    66	//       | Reserved    | 0x7D, 0x7C,  | HeapTypeCode        |
    67	//       | (Padding)   |   (numtype)  | 0x00, 0x40,         |    Type index
    68	//  code |             | 0x7B,        | 0x70, 0x6F,         |    (uint32_t)
    69	//       |             |   (vectype)  | (func-ref proposal) |
    70	//       |   1st:      | 0x78, 0x77,  | 0x73, 0x72, 0x71,   |

    72	//       |             | 0x64, 0x63   | 0x6B, 0x6A,         |
    73	//       |             |   (reftype)  |    (GC proposal)    |
    74	//       |             |              | 0x69                |
    75	//       |             |              | (Exception handling proposal)
    76	// -----------------------------------------------------------------------------
    77	// In order to compress the various value type definitions into uint64_t length,
    78	// WasmEdge implements the ValType class for extending the value types.
    79	// As the definitions in the typed function references and GC proposal, the
    80	// `FuncRef` and `ExternRef` are reinterpreted as the `ref.null` types,
    81	// respectively. Therefore, WasmEdge hendles them into `ref null func` and `ref
    82	// null extern` in the ValType classes.
    83	
    84	/// ValType class definition.
    85	class ValType {
    86	public:
    87	  // Note: The padding bytes are reserved and should not be written.
    88	  ValType() noexcept = default;
    89	  // General constructors for initializing data.
    90	  ValType(TypeCode C, TypeCode HT, uint32_t I) noexcept {
    91	    Inner.Data.Externalize = 0;
    92	    Inner.Data.Code = C;
    93	    Inner.Data.HTCode = HT;
    94	    Inner.Data.Idx = I;
    95	  }
    96	  ValType(const std::array<uint8_t, 8> R) noexcept {
    97	    std::copy_n(R.cbegin(), 8, Inner.Raw);
    98	  }
    99	  // Constructor for the value type codes without heap type immediates.
   100	  ValType(TypeCode C) noexcept {
   101	    Inner.Data.Externalize = 0;
   102	    Inner.Data.Idx = 0;
   103	    switch (C) {
   104	    case TypeCode::I32:
   105	    case TypeCode::I64:
   106	    case TypeCode::F32:
   107	    case TypeCode::F64:
   108	      // Number type
   109	    case TypeCode::V128:
   110	      // Vector type
   111	    case TypeCode::I8:
   112	    case TypeCode::I16:
   113	      // Packed type
   114	      Inner.Data.Code = C;
   115	      Inner.Data.HTCode = TypeCode::Epsilon;
   116	      break;
   117	    case TypeCode::NullExnRef:
   118	    case TypeCode::NullFuncRef:
   119	    case TypeCode::NullExternRef:
   120	    case TypeCode::NullRef:
   121	    case TypeCode::FuncRef:
   122	    case TypeCode::ExternRef:
   123	    case TypeCode::AnyRef:
   124	    case TypeCode::EqRef:
   125	    case TypeCode::I31Ref:
   126	    case TypeCode::StructRef:
   127	    case TypeCode::ArrayRef:
   128	    case TypeCode::ExnRef:
   129	      // Abstract heap type
   130	      Inner.Data.Code = TypeCode::RefNull;
   131	      Inner.Data.HTCode = C;
   132	      break;
   133	    case TypeCode::Ref:
   134	    case TypeCode::RefNull:
   135	      // Reference type with heap immediates should use the constructors below.
   136	    default:
   137	      assumingUnreachable();
   138	    }
   139	  }
   140	  // Constructor for the value type with abs heap type in reference type.
   141	  ValType(TypeCode C, TypeCode HT) noexcept {
   142	    Inner.Data.Externalize = 0;
   143	    Inner.Data.Code = C;
   144	    Inner.Data.HTCode = HT;
   145	    Inner.Data.Idx = 0;
   146	    assuming(isAbsHeapType());
   147	  }
   148	  // Constructor for the value type with type index in reference type.
   149	  ValType(TypeCode C, uint32_t I) noexcept {
   150	    Inner.Data.Externalize = 0;
   151	    Inner.Data.Code = C;
   152	    Inner.Data.HTCode = TypeCode::TypeIndex;
   153	    Inner.Data.Idx = I;
   154	    assuming(isRefType());
   155	  }
   156	
   157	  friend bool operator==(const ValType &LHS, const ValType &RHS) noexcept {
   158	    return (LHS.Inner.Data.Code == RHS.Inner.Data.Code) &&
   159	           (LHS.Inner.Data.HTCode == RHS.Inner.Data.HTCode) &&
   160	           (LHS.Inner.Data.Idx == RHS.Inner.Data.Idx);
   161	  }
   162	  friend bool operator!=(const ValType &LHS, const ValType &RHS) noexcept {
   163	    return !(LHS == RHS);
   164	  }

   167	  TypeCode getHeapTypeCode() const noexcept { return Inner.Data.HTCode; }
   168	  uint32_t getTypeIndex() const noexcept { return Inner.Data.Idx; }

TypeCode Executor::toBottomType(
    const Runtime::Instance::ModuleInstance *ModInst, const ValType &Type) const {
  if (Type.isRefType()) {
    if (Type.isAbsHeapType()) {
      switch (Type.getHeapTypeCode()) {
      case TypeCode::NullFuncRef:
      case TypeCode::FuncRef:
        return TypeCode::NullFuncRef;
      case TypeCode::NullExternRef:
      case TypeCode::ExternRef:
        return TypeCode::NullExternRef;
      case TypeCode::NullRef:
      case TypeCode::AnyRef:
      case TypeCode::EqRef:
      case TypeCode::I31Ref:
      case TypeCode::StructRef:
      case TypeCode::ArrayRef:
        return TypeCode::NullRef;
      case TypeCode::NullExnRef:
      case TypeCode::ExnRef:
        return TypeCode::NullExnRef;
      default:
        assumingUnreachable();
      }
    } else {
      const auto &CompType =
          (*ModInst->getType(Type.getTypeIndex()))->getCompositeType();
      if (CompType.isFunc()) {
        return TypeCode::NullFuncRef;
      } else {
        return TypeCode::NullRef;
      }
    }
  } else {
    return Type.getCode();
  }
}

   435	  if (Type.isRefType()) {
   436	    if (Type.isAbsHeapType()) {
   437	      switch (Type.getHeapTypeCode()) {
   438	      case TypeCode::NullFuncRef:
   439	      case TypeCode::FuncRef:
   440	        return TypeCode::NullFuncRef;
   441	      case TypeCode::NullExternRef:
   442	      case TypeCode::ExternRef:
   443	        return TypeCode::NullExternRef;
   444	      case TypeCode::NullRef:
   445	      case TypeCode::AnyRef:
   446	      case TypeCode::EqRef:
   447	      case TypeCode::I31Ref:
   448	      case TypeCode::StructRef:
   449	      case TypeCode::ArrayRef:
   450	        return TypeCode::NullRef;
   451	      case TypeCode::NullExnRef:
   452	      case TypeCode::ExnRef:
   453	        return TypeCode::NullExnRef;
   454	      default:
   455	        assumingUnreachable();
   456	      }
   457	    } else {
   458	      const auto &CompType =
   459	          (*ModInst->getType(Type.getTypeIndex()))->getCompositeType();
   460	      if (CompType.isFunc()) {
   461	        return TypeCode::NullFuncRef;
   462	      } else {
   463	        return TypeCode::NullRef;
   464	      }
   465	    }
   466	  } else {
   467	    return Type.getCode();
   468	  }
   469	}
   470

   472	                               const ValType &Type) const noexcept {
   473	  if (Type.isNumType()) {

+TypeCode Executor::toBottomType(
